# python3 - <<EOF
import os

files_to_patch = [
    "HelloApp_Decompiled/smali_classes5/com/taobao/accs/utl/AdapterUtilityImpl.smali",
    "HelloApp_Decompiled/smali_classes5/com/taobao/accs/utl/UtilityImpl.smali"
]

patch_code = """
.method public static getDeviceId(Landroid/content/Context;)Ljava/lang/String;
    .locals 1
    const-string v0, "GRATECH_GHOST_403_SULIMAN"
    return-object v0
.end method
"""

for file_path in files_to_patch:
    if os.path.exists(file_path):
        with open(file_path, 'r') as f:
            lines = f.readlines()

        new_lines = []
        skip = False
        for line in lines:
            if ".method public static getDeviceId(Landroid/content/Context;)Ljava/lang/String;" in line:
                new_lines.append(patch_code)
                skip = True
            elif skip and ".end method" in line:
                skip = False
                continue
            if not skip:
                new_lines.append(line)

        with open(file_path, 'w') as f:
            f.writelines(new_lines)
        print(f"[*] Patched: {file_path}")
    else:
        print(f"[!] File not found: {file_path}")

Copilot

   7  

   

   Entra

  
    Cloud Shell   Bash  Azure CLI ( PowerShell)   Connect-AzAccount / Get-Az*  .
    gratech.sa    (gratechk sa)       (gratechx).

 :   Bash/Azure CLI         gratech.sa /     ( )            .

 :    Entra ID (Azure AD)      UPN/ProxyAddress/Email.     UPNs     *.onmicrosoft.com  .

    Cloud Shell (Bash + Azure CLI)
   .      Cloud Shell  Enter.




Shell
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

# ==========================
#  ( )
# ==========================
DOMAIN="gratech.sa"
KEEP_TENANT="352ade02-f27a-4888-bb45-89360dad9423"   #    Gratechx 
GRAPH="https://graph.microsoft.com"

echo "==>      Azure CLI..."
az account show >/dev/null 2>&1 || az login --use-device-code 1>/dev/null

echo "==>    ..."
mapfile -t TENANTS < <(az account tenant list --query "[].tenantId" -o tsv)

if [ ${#TENANTS[@]} -eq 0 ]; then
  echo "      ."
  exit 1
fi

FOUND_TENANT=""
echo "==>      : $DOMAIN"
for T in "${TENANTS[@]}"; do
  az account tenant set --tenant "$T" 1>/dev/null
  #     
  if az rest --resource $GRAPH -m GET -u "$GRAPH/v1.0/domains/$DOMAIN" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    FOUND_TENANT="$T"
    echo "      : $FOUND_TENANT"
    break
  fi
done

if [ -z "$FOUND_TENANT" ]; then
  echo "      $DOMAIN       ."
  echo "              ."
  exit 0
fi

if [ "$FOUND_TENANT" = "$KEEP_TENANT" ]; then
  echo "  $DOMAIN         (KEEP_TENANT).   ."
  exit 0
fi

echo "==>      ..."
az account tenant set --tenant "$FOUND_TENANT" 1>/dev/null

#    onmicrosoft.com    UPNs
DEFAULT_ONMS=$(az rest --resource $GRAPH -m GET -u "$GRAPH/v1.0/domains" \
  --query "value[?ends_with(id,'onmicrosoft.com')].id | [0]" -o tsv)

if [ -z "$DEFAULT_ONMS" ]; then
  echo "     *.onmicrosoft.com   ."
  exit 1
fi
echo "==>    : $DEFAULT_ONMS"

echo "==>        (Users/Groups/Apps/ServicePrincipals)..."

# 1)   UPN  ProxyAddresses   
echo "==>       UPN..."
mapfile -t USERS_UPN < <(az rest --resource $GRAPH -m GET \
  -u "$GRAPH/v1.0/users?\$select=id,userPrincipalName&\$filter=endswith(userPrincipalName,'@$DOMAIN')" \
  --query "value[].{id:id,upn:userPrincipalName}" -o tsv || true)

echo "==>      ProxyAddresses  ..."
mapfile -t USERS_PROXY < <(az rest --resource $GRAPH -m GET \
  -u "$GRAPH/v1.0/users?\$select=id,proxyAddresses,userPrincipalName" \
  --query "value[?proxyAddresses[?contains(@,'@$DOMAIN')]].{id:id,upn:userPrincipalName}" -o tsv || true)

#   ( )
declare -A USER_IDS=()
for line in "${USERS_UPN[@]}"; do
  uid=$(awk '{print $1}' <<<"$line")
  upn=$(awk '{print $2}' <<<"$line")
  USER_IDS["$uid"]="$upn"
done
for line in "${USERS_PROXY[@]}"; do
  uid=$(awk '{print $1}' <<<"$line")
  upn=$(awk '{print $2}' <<<"$line")
  USER_IDS["$uid"]="$upn"
done

echo "==>     : ${#USER_IDS[@]}"

# 2) ()        (   Exchange/Entra ID P1/P2)
#   
GROUPS_CNT=$(az rest --resource $GRAPH -m GET \
  -u "$GRAPH/v1.0/groups?\$select=id,mail&\$filter=endswith(mail,'@$DOMAIN')" \
  --query "value | length(@)" -o tsv || echo 0)
echo "==>         : $GROUPS_CNT"

# 3) /Service Principals    Reply/Identifier URIs         
APPS_CNT=$(az rest --resource $GRAPH -m GET \
  -u "$GRAPH/v1.0/applications?\$count=true" --headers "ConsistencyLevel=eventual" \
  --query "length(value[?contains(identifierUris, '://') && contains(join('',identifierUris),'$DOMAIN')])" -o tsv || echo 0)
SPN_CNT=$(az rest --resource $GRAPH -m GET \
  -u "$GRAPH/v1.0/servicePrincipals?\$count=true" --headers "ConsistencyLevel=eventual" \
  --query "length(value[?contains(homepage, '$DOMAIN') || contains(loginUrl, '$DOMAIN')])" -o tsv || echo 0)
echo "==>    : $APPS_CNT | Service Principals: $SPN_CNT ( )"

# ==========================
#  UPN  ( )  @DOMAIN  @DEFAULT_ONMS
# ==========================
if [ ${#USER_IDS[@]} -gt 0 ]; then
  echo "==>   UPNs     ..."
  for uid in "${!USER_IDS[@]}"; do
    old_upn="${USER_IDS[$uid]}"
    new_upn="${old_upn%@*}@$DEFAULT_ONMS"
    if [ "$old_upn" = "$new_upn" ]; then
      continue
    fi
    echo "   - $old_upn  -->  $new_upn"
    az rest --resource $GRAPH -m PATCH \
      -u "$GRAPH/v1.0/users/$uid" \
      --headers "Content-Type=application/json" \
      --body "{\"userPrincipalName\":\"$new_upn\"}" >/dev/null
  done
  echo "==>   UPNs  ."
else
  echo "==>      UPN."
fi

# :   Exchange Online           EXO PowerShell.
#         .

echo "==>      : $FOUND_TENANT"
if az rest --resource $GRAPH -m DELETE -u "$GRAPH/v1.0/domains/$DOMAIN" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
  echo "    $DOMAIN   $FOUND_TENANT ."
else
  echo "    .      :"
  echo "   -      User/Group/Contact  UPN/mail/ProxyAddress  $DOMAIN."
  echo "   -     federated domain  Email routing."
  echo "   -    Exchange Online mailboxes   primary SMTP."
  echo ""
  echo "  :"
  echo " -    : $GROUPS_CNT"
  echo " -    (  ): Apps=$APPS_CNT, SPNs=$SPN_CNT"
  echo ""
  echo "           ."
  exit 1
fi

# ==========================
#  :    Gratechx (KEEP_TENANT)   
# ==========================
echo "==>     (KEEP_TENANT)   ..."
az account tenant set --tenant "$KEEP_TENANT" 1>/dev/null

echo "==>      (   )..."
if az rest --resource $GRAPH -m GET -u "$GRAPH/v1.0/domains/$DOMAIN" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
  echo "  $DOMAIN     ."
else
  az rest --resource $GRAPH -m POST -u "$GRAPH/v1.0/domains" \
    --headers "Content-Type=application/json" \
    --body "{\"id\":\"$DOMAIN\"}" >/dev/null
  echo "      Entra ID."
fi

echo "==>    TXT ..."
TXT=$(az rest --resource $GRAPH -m GET -u "$GRAPH/v1.0/domains/$DOMAIN/verificationDnsRecords" \
      --query "value[?recordType=='Txt'].{name:label,txt:text,ttl:ttl}.text(@)" -o tsv 2>/dev/null | head -n1 || true)

LABEL=$(az rest --resource $GRAPH -m GET -u "$GRAPH/v1.0/domains/$DOMAIN/verificationDnsRecords" \
      --query "value[?recordType=='Txt'].[label]" -o tsv 2>/dev/null | head -n1 || true)

TTL=$(az rest --resource $GRAPH -m GET -u "$GRAPH/v1.0/domains/$DOMAIN/verificationDnsRecords" \
      --query "value[?recordType=='Txt'].[ttl]" -o tsv 2>/dev/null | head -n1 || echo 3600)

if [ -n "$TXT" ] && [ -n "$LABEL" ]; then
  echo "==>    TXT  DNS Zone  :"
  echo "    Name : $LABEL"
  echo "    Type : TXT"
  echo "    TTL  : ${TTL:-3600}"
  echo "    Value: $TXT"
else
  echo "     TXT .      Entra ID > Custom domain names."
fi

echo "==>   TXT   ..."
if az rest --resource $GRAPH -m POST -u "$GRAPH/v1.0/domains/$DOMAIN/verify" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
  echo "     $DOMAIN    ."
else
  echo "         DNS     :"
  echo "    az rest --resource $GRAPH -m POST -u \"$GRAPH/v1.0/domains/$DOMAIN/verify\""
fi

echo "."
  

       Cloud Shell.

     (KEEP_TENANT = 352ade02-f27a-4888-bb45-89360dad9423)   UPNs     .

Shell
#  
RG="gratech-cometx_group"
ZONE="gratech.sa"
RECORD_NAME="_dnsauth"          #   LABEL      
TXT_VALUE="v=verifydomain=XXXXXXXXXXXX"  #     

# / TXT
az network dns record-set txt create -g "$RG" -z "$ZONE" -n "$RECORD_NAME" --ttl 3600
az network dns record-set txt add-record -g "$RG" -z "$ZONE" -n "$RECORD_NAME" -v "$TXT_VALUE" || true

#  
az rest --resource https://graph.microsoft.com -m POST -u "https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/domains/$ZONE/verify"

Azure DNS is a hosting service for DNS domains that provides name resolution by using Microsoft Azure infrastructure. By hosting your domains in Azure, you can manage your DNS records by using the same credentials, APIs, tools, and billing as your other Azure services.

Add DNS record sets
Begin hosting your domain in Azure DNS by adding record sets. A record set is a collection of records in a zone that have the same name and are the same type.
Import record sets from file
You have the option to import your zone directly using the import utility. This utility offers a rapid, dependable, and convenient method for transferring DNS zone data into or out of Azure DNS.
Access control
View your level of access to DNS zone. Review the level of access a user, group, service principal, or managed identity has to this DNS zone.
Azure DNS Documentation
For detail understanding of Azure DNS, refer to the documentation.

        // ============================================

        // AI Input
        const aiInput = document.getElementById('aiInput');
        aiInput.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
            if (e.key === 'Enter' &amp;&amp; !e.shiftKey) {
                e.preventDefault();
                sendAIMessage();
            }
        });

        aiInput.addEventListener('input', function () {
            this.style.height = 'auto';
            this.style.height = Math.min(this.scrollHeight, 120) + 'px';
        });

        function sendAIMessage() {
            const input = document.getElementById('aiInput');
            const message = input.value.trim();
            if (!message) return;

            // Add user message
            addMessage(message, 'user');
            input.value = '';
            input.style.height = 'auto';

            // Simulate AI response
            setTimeout(() =&gt; {
                const responses = [
                    '     . :  .',
                    '  :   .    .',
                    '  ...   100%.',
                    '    .  .  .',
                    ' Three-Lobe  .    '
                ];
                addMessage(responses[Math.floor(Math.random() * responses.length)], 'system');
            }, 800);
        }

        function addMessage(text, type) {
            const chat = document.getElementById('aiChat');
            const msg = document.createElement('div');
            msg.className = `ai-message ${type}`;

            const icon = type === 'system' ? '' : '';
            const sender = type === 'system' ? 'Comet-X' : '';

            msg.innerHTML = `
                &lt;div class="ai-message-header"&gt;
                    &lt;span&gt;${icon}&lt;/span&gt;
                    &lt;span&gt;${sender}&lt;/span&gt;
                &lt;/div&gt;
                &lt;div class="ai-message-content"&gt;${text}&lt;/div&gt;
            `;

            chat.appendChild(msg);
            chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight;
        }

        // ============================================

        function search() {

            if (query) {
                window.open(`https://www.google.com/search?q=${encodeURIComponent(query)}`, '_blank');
            }
        }

        document.getElementById('searchInput').addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
            if (e.key === 'Enter') search();
        });

            // Electron only

        function maximizeWindow() {

                document.exitFullscreen();

                document.documentElement.requestFullscreen();
            }
        }

        // ============================================
        // Keyboard Shortcuts
        // ============================================
        document.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
            // Ctrl+Shift+C - Toggle AI
            if (e.ctrlKey &amp;&amp; e.shiftKey &amp;&amp; e.key === 'C') {
                e.preventDefault();
                toggleAI();
            }
            // Ctrl+T - New Tab
            if (e.ctrlKey &amp;&amp; e.key === 't') {
                e.preventDefault();
                newTab();
            }
            // Ctrl+L - Focus URL
            if (e.ctrlKey &amp;&amp; e.key === 'l') {
                e.preventDefault();
                document.getElementById('urlInput').focus();
                document.getElementById('urlInput').select();
            }
            // Escape - Close panels
            if (e.key === 'Escape') {
                closeVision();
                document.getElementById('aiSidebar').classList.remove('open');
            }
        });

        let currentLang = 'ar';

        function setLang(lang) {
            currentLang = lang;
            const t = translations[lang];
            const isRTL = lang === 'ar';

            // Update direction
            document.documentElement.lang = lang;
            document.documentElement.dir = isRTL ? 'rtl' : 'ltr';
            document.body.style.direction = isRTL ? 'rtl' : 'ltr';

            // Update texts
            document.querySelector('.brand-tagline').textContent = t.tagline;
            document.querySelector('.search-input').placeholder = t.searchPlaceholder;
            document.querySelector('#aiInput').placeholder = t.inputPlaceholder;

            // Update badges
            const badges = document.querySelectorAll('.badge');
            if (badges.length &gt;= 4) {
                badges[0].textContent = t.local;
                badges[1].textContent = t.neutral;
                badges[2].textContent = t.vision;
                badges[3].textContent = t.threeLobe;
            }

            // Update language buttons
            document.querySelectorAll('.lang-btn').forEach(btn =&gt; {
                btn.classList.remove('active');
            });
            document.querySelector(`.lang-btn[onclick="setLang('${lang}')"]`).classList.add('active');

            // Update i18n elements
            document.querySelectorAll('[data-i18n]').forEach(el =&gt; {
                const key = el.getAttribute('data-i18n');
                if (t[key]) el.textContent = t[key];
            });

            // Save preference
            localStorage.setItem('cometx-lang', lang);
        }

        // Load saved language
        const savedLang = localStorage.getItem('cometx-lang');
        if (savedLang &amp;&amp; translations[savedLang]) {
            setLang(savedLang);
        }

    &lt;script src="src/ai/sovereign-ai.js"&gt;&lt;/script&gt;
    &lt;script&gt;
        const sovereignAI = new SovereignAI();
        
        function openSovereignAI(lobe) {
            sovereignAI.currentModel = MODELS[lobe === 'cognitive' ? 'claude' : 'gpt4'];
            document.getElementById('ai-panel').classList.add('active');
            document.querySelector('.ai-chat-title').textContent = sovereignAI.currentModel.icon + ' ' + sovereignAI.currentModel.name;
        }
        
        // Auto-detect language from input
        document.querySelector('.ai-input')?.addEventListener('input', function(e) {
            const text = e.target.value;
            const arabicRegex = /[\u0600-\u06FF]/;
            if (arabicRegex.test(text)) {
                sovereignAI.currentLang = 'ar';
            } else {
                sovereignAI.currentLang = 'en';
            }
        });
        
        // Override sendMessage to use real AI
        const originalSendMessage = window.sendMessage;
        window.sendMessage = async function() {
            const input = document.querySelector('.ai-input');
            const message = input.value.trim();
            if (!message) return;
            
            // Add user message
            addMessage(message, 'user');
            input.value = '';
            
            // Show typing indicator
            const typingDiv = document.createElement('div');
            typingDiv.className = 'ai-message comet typing';
            typingDiv.innerHTML = '&lt;div class="message-content"&gt; ...&lt;/div&gt;';
            document.querySelector('.ai-chat-messages').appendChild(typingDiv);
            
            try {
                const response = await sovereignAI.chat(message);
                typingDiv.remove();
                if (response.choices &amp;&amp; response.choices[0]) {
                    addMessage(response.choices[0].message.content, 'comet');
                } else {
                    addMessage('  .   .', 'comet');
                }
            } catch (err) {
                typingDiv.remove();
                addMessage('  .   .', 'comet');
            }
        };

Shell
#==============================
# 0)  
#==============================
RG_DNS="gratech-dns-rg"
ZONE="gratech.sa"
APP_RG="gratechx-auto-rg"
APP_NAME="gratech-demo"      #     
DOMAIN="gratech.sa"
SUBDOMAIN="@"
WEBAPP_HOST="$DOMAIN"

#==============================
# 1)  Custom Domain  App Service
#==============================
echo "   TXT    ..."
az network dns record-set txt add-record \
  --resource-group "$RG_DNS" \
  --zone-name "$ZONE" \
  --record-set-name "asuid.$DOMAIN" \
  --value "$(az webapp config hostname get-external-ip --resource-group $APP_RG --name $APP_NAME)"

echo "  10    DNS..."
sleep 10

echo "    App Service..."
az webapp config hostname add \
  --hostname "$WEBAPP_HOST" \
  --resource-group "$APP_RG" \
  --webapp-name "$APP_NAME"

#==============================
# 2)  SSL 
#==============================
echo " / SSL   Azure Managed Certificate..."
az webapp config ssl create \
  --resource-group "$APP_RG" \
  --name "$APP_NAME" \
  --hostname "$WEBAPP_HOST"

CERT=$(az webapp config ssl list --resource-group $APP_RG --query "[?friendlyName=='$WEBAPP_HOST'].thumbprint" -o tsv)

echo "   ..."
az webapp config ssl bind \
  --certificate-thumbprint "$CERT" \
  --ssl-type SNI \
  --resource-group "$APP_RG" \
  --name "$APP_NAME"

echo "      +  SSL   !"

Ran terminal command: $domains = @("tikhak.com", "faceline.live", "hiloconn.com", "chathot.me")
foreach ($domain in $domains) {
    Write-Host "========== WHOIS: $domain ==========" -ForegroundColor Cyan
    try {
        $result = Invoke-RestMethod -Uri "https://whois.freeaiapi.xyz/?name=$domain" -TimeoutSec 10
        $result | ConvertTo-Json -Depth 5
    } catch {
        Write-Host "Using nslookup fallback..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
        nslookup $domain
    }
    Write-Host ""
}

I've created copilot-instructions.md for this fraud investigation project.

**What the instructions cover:**
1. **Project overview** - Identifies this as a fraud investigation case with decompiled Android evidence

About this app
Welcome to Hilo! Its easy to connect with people who share your interests anytime.
Exploring diverse cultures and making new friends has never been simpler. Come expand your social circle and have fun together!

Group Chat
Join your favorite groups and connect with fellow enthusiasts from around the world!

Interesting Social Games
Enjoy challenging friends with a variety of fun games, including Carrom, Ludo, Uno, Snack, and many more! Experience the thrill of gaming and socializing in one place!

Group Play & Voice Chat
Team up with friends in group games and compete to see whos the best! Support real-time voice chat during gameplay to stay connected with your squad.

Fun Interaction
A wide range of creative gifts and emoticons make your chats more lively and engaging.

Rewarding Activities
Participate in various in-app activities to earn exciting in-game rewards.

Safe & Friendly Community
- If you don't want to be disturbed, you can lock the group.
- Built-in content moderation system filters inappropriate messages and behaviors.
- Report function is available for users to flag any violations easily.

If you have any questions or suggestions, feel free to contact us via email: hiloassist@gmail.com.
Updated on
Jan 9, 2026
Data safety
Safety starts with understanding how developers collect and share your data. Data privacy and security practices may vary based on your use, region, and age. The developer provided this information and may update it over time.

About this app
Welcome to Hilo! Its easy to connect with people who share your interests anytime.
Exploring diverse cultures and making new friends has never been simpler. Come expand your social circle and have fun together!

Group Chat
Join your favorite groups and connect with fellow enthusiasts from around the world!

Interesting Social Games
Enjoy challenging friends with a variety of fun games, including Carrom, Ludo, Uno, Snack, and many more! Experience the thrill of gaming and socializing in one place!

Group Play & Voice Chat
Team up with friends in group games and compete to see whos the best! Support real-time voice chat during gameplay to stay connected with your squad.

Fun Interaction
A wide range of creative gifts and emoticons make your chats more lively and engaging.

Rewarding Activities
Participate in various in-app activities to earn exciting in-game rewards.

Safe & Friendly Community
- If you don't want to be disturbed, you can lock the group.
- Built-in content moderation system filters inappropriate messages and behaviors.
- Report function is available for users to flag any violations easily.

If you have any questions or suggestions, feel free to contact us via email: hiloassist@gmail.com.

    <script>
        // ===== MUSIC CONTROL =====
        let isPlaying = false;
        const audio = document.getElementById('bg-music');
        const musicBtn = document.getElementById('music-btn');
        const soundWave = document.getElementById('sound-wave');
        
        function enterSite() {
            // Hide intro overlay
            document.getElementById('intro-overlay').style.display = 'none';
            // Auto-play music
            playMusic();
        }
        
        function playMusic() {
            audio.play().then(() => {
                isPlaying = true;
                musicBtn.textContent = '';
                soundWave.classList.remove('paused');
            }).catch(err => {
                console.log('Autoplay blocked:', err);
            });
        }
        
        function toggleMusic() {
            if (isPlaying) {
                audio.pause();
                musicBtn.textContent = '';
                soundWave.classList.add('paused');
            } else {
                audio.play();
                musicBtn.textContent = '';
                soundWave.classList.remove('paused');
            }
            isPlaying = !isPlaying;
        }
        
        // ===== LANGUAGE SWITCHER =====
        function setLang(lang) {
            // Update direction
            document.documentElement.dir = lang === 'ar' ? 'rtl' : 'ltr';
            document.documentElement.lang = lang;
            
            // Update buttons
            document.querySelectorAll('.lang-btn').forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
            event.target.classList.add('active');
            
            // Update all translatable elements
            document.querySelectorAll('[data-' + lang + ']').forEach(el => {
                el.textContent = el.getAttribute('data-' + lang);
            });
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        // ===== WEB AUDIO API - Generate Epic Music =====
        let audioContext;
        let isPlaying = false;
        let oscillators = [];
        let gainNode;
        
        function createEpicMusic() {
            audioContext = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
            gainNode = audioContext.createGain();
            gainNode.connect(audioContext.destination);
            gainNode.gain.value = 0.3;
            
            // Epic chord progression (Dm - Bb - F - C)
            const chords = [
                [146.83, 174.61, 220.00], // Dm
                [116.54, 146.83, 174.61], // Bb
                [174.61, 220.00, 261.63], // F
                [130.81, 164.81, 196.00]  // C
            ];
            
            let chordIndex = 0;
            
            function playChord() {
                // Stop previous oscillators
                oscillators.forEach(osc => {
                    try { osc.stop(); } catch(e) {}
                });
                oscillators = [];
                
                if (!isPlaying) return;
                
                const chord = chords[chordIndex % chords.length];
                
                chord.forEach((freq, i) => {
                    const osc = audioContext.createOscillator();
                    const oscGain = audioContext.createGain();
                    
                    osc.type = i === 0 ? 'sawtooth' : 'triangle';
                    osc.frequency.value = freq;
                    
                    oscGain.gain.value = 0.15;
                    oscGain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.01, audioContext.currentTime + 1.8);
                    
                    osc.connect(oscGain);
                    oscGain.connect(gainNode);
                    osc.start();
                    
                    oscillators.push(osc);
                });
                
                // Bass note
                const bass = audioContext.createOscillator();
                const bassGain = audioContext.createGain();
                bass.type = 'sine';
                bass.frequency.value = chord[0] / 2;
                bassGain.gain.value = 0.2;
                bass.connect(bassGain);
                bassGain.connect(gainNode);
                bass.start();
                oscillators.push(bass);
                
                // Drum beat
                playDrum();
                
                chordIndex++;
                if (isPlaying) {
                    setTimeout(playChord, 2000);
                }
            }
            
            function playDrum() {
                const noise = audioContext.createBufferSource();
                const noiseBuffer = audioContext.createBuffer(1, audioContext.sampleRate * 0.1, audioContext.sampleRate);
                const output = noiseBuffer.getChannelData(0);
                
                for (let i = 0; i < noiseBuffer.length; i++) {
                    output[i] = Math.random() * 2 - 1;
                }
                
                noise.buffer = noiseBuffer;
                
                const noiseGain = audioContext.createGain();
                noiseGain.gain.value = 0.3;
                noiseGain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.01, audioContext.currentTime + 0.1);
                
                const filter = audioContext.createBiquadFilter();
                filter.type = 'lowpass';
                filter.frequency.value = 150;
                
                noise.connect(filter);
                filter.connect(noiseGain);
                noiseGain.connect(audioContext.destination);
                noise.start();
            }
            
            playChord();
        }
        
        function enterSite() {
            document.getElementById('intro-overlay').style.display = 'none';
            isPlaying = true;
            createEpicMusic();
            document.getElementById('music-btn').textContent = '';
            document.getElementById('sound-wave').classList.remove('paused');
        }
        
        function toggleMusic() {
            if (isPlaying) {
                isPlaying = false;
                oscillators.forEach(osc => {
                    try { osc.stop(); } catch(e) {}
                });
                document.getElementById('music-btn').textContent = '';
                document.getElementById('sound-wave').classList.add('paused');
            } else {
                isPlaying = true;
                createEpicMusic();
                document.getElementById('music-btn').textContent = '';
                document.getElementById('sound-wave').classList.remove('paused');
            }
        }
        
        // ===== LANGUAGE SWITCHER =====
        function setLang(lang) {
            document.documentElement.dir = lang === 'ar' ? 'rtl' : 'ltr';
            document.documentElement.lang = lang;
            
            document.querySelectorAll('.lang-btn').forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
            event.target.classList.add('active');
            
            document.querySelectorAll('[data-' + lang + ']').forEach(el => {
                el.textContent = el.getAttribute('data-' + lang);
            });
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>

GitHub Copilot: You can change VS Code to light mode in several ways:

## Quick Methods

1. **Keyboard Shortcut**: Press `Ctrl+K Ctrl+T` to open the theme picker, then select a light theme like "Light Modern" or "Light+"

2. **Command Palette**: Press `Ctrl+Shift+P`, type "Color Theme", select **Preferences: Color Theme**, and choose a light theme

## Via Settings

1. Press `Ctrl+,` to open Settings
2. Search for "Color Theme"
3. Select a light theme from the dropdown under **Workbench: Color Theme**

## Popular Light Themes
- **Light Modern** (default light theme)
- **Light+** (classic VS Code light)
- **Quiet Light**
- **Solarized Light**

foreach ($domain in $domains) {
    Write-Host "========== WHOIS: $domain ==========" -ForegroundColor Cyan
    try {
        $result = Invoke-RestMethod -Uri "https://whois.freeaiapi.xyz/?name=$domain" -TimeoutSec 10
        $result | ConvertTo-Json -Depth 5
    } catch {
        Write-Host "Using nslookup fallback..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
        nslookup $domain
    }
    Write-Host ""
}

About this app
Welcome to Hilo! Its easy to connect with people who share your interests anytime.
Exploring diverse cultures and making new friends has never been simpler. Come expand your social circle and have fun together!

Group Chat
Join your favorite groups and connect with fellow enthusiasts from around the world!

Interesting Social Games
Enjoy challenging friends with a variety of fun games, including Carrom, Ludo, Uno, Snack, and many more! Experience the thrill of gaming and socializing in one place!

Group Play & Voice Chat
Team up with friends in group games and compete to see whos the best! Support real-time voice chat during gameplay to stay connected with your squad.

Fun Interaction
A wide range of creative gifts and emoticons make your chats more lively and engaging.

Rewarding Activities
Participate in various in-app activities to earn exciting in-game rewards.

Safe & Friendly Community
- If you don't want to be disturbed, you can lock the group.
- Built-in content moderation system filters inappropriate messages and behaviors.
- Report function is available for users to flag any violations easily.

If you have any questions or suggestions, feel free to contact us via email: hiloassist@gmail.com.

    <script>
        // ===== MUSIC CONTROL =====
        let isPlaying = false;
        const audio = document.getElementById('bg-music');
        const musicBtn = document.getElementById('music-btn');
        const soundWave = document.getElementById('sound-wave');
        
        function enterSite() {
            // Hide intro overlay
            document.getElementById('intro-overlay').style.display = 'none';
            // Auto-play music
            playMusic();
        }
        
        function playMusic() {
            audio.play().then(() => {
                isPlaying = true;
                musicBtn.textContent = '';
                soundWave.classList.remove('paused');
            }).catch(err => {
                console.log('Autoplay blocked:', err);
            });
        }
        
        function toggleMusic() {
            if (isPlaying) {
                audio.pause();
                musicBtn.textContent = '';
                soundWave.classList.add('paused');
            } else {
                audio.play();
                musicBtn.textContent = '';
                soundWave.classList.remove('paused');
            }
            isPlaying = !isPlaying;
        }
        
        // ===== LANGUAGE SWITCHER =====
        function setLang(lang) {
            // Update direction
            document.documentElement.dir = lang === 'ar' ? 'rtl' : 'ltr';
            document.documentElement.lang = lang;
            
            // Update buttons
            document.querySelectorAll('.lang-btn').forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
            event.target.classList.add('active');
            
            // Update all translatable elements
            document.querySelectorAll('[data-' + lang + ']').forEach(el => {
                el.textContent = el.getAttribute('data-' + lang);
            });
        }
    </script>

    <script>
        // ===== WEB AUDIO API - Generate Epic Music =====
        let audioContext;
        let isPlaying = false;
        let oscillators = [];
        let gainNode;
        
        function createEpicMusic() {
            audioContext = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
            gainNode = audioContext.createGain();
            gainNode.connect(audioContext.destination);
            gainNode.gain.value = 0.3;
            
            // Epic chord progression (Dm - Bb - F - C)
            const chords = [
                [146.83, 174.61, 220.00], // Dm
                [116.54, 146.83, 174.61], // Bb
                [174.61, 220.00, 261.63], // F
                [130.81, 164.81, 196.00]  // C
            ];
            
            let chordIndex = 0;
            
            function playChord() {
                // Stop previous oscillators
                oscillators.forEach(osc => {
                    try { osc.stop(); } catch(e) {}
                });
                oscillators = [];
                
                if (!isPlaying) return;
                
                const chord = chords[chordIndex % chords.length];
                
                chord.forEach((freq, i) => {
                    const osc = audioContext.createOscillator();
                    const oscGain = audioContext.createGain();
                    
                    osc.type = i === 0 ? 'sawtooth' : 'triangle';
                    osc.frequency.value = freq;
                    
                    oscGain.gain.value = 0.15;
                    oscGain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.01, audioContext.currentTime + 1.8);
                    
                    osc.connect(oscGain);
                    oscGain.connect(gainNode);
                    osc.start();
                    
                    oscillators.push(osc);
                });
                
                // Bass note
                const bass = audioContext.createOscillator();
                const bassGain = audioContext.createGain();
                bass.type = 'sine';
                bass.frequency.value = chord[0] / 2;
                bassGain.gain.value = 0.2;
                bass.connect(bassGain);
                bassGain.connect(gainNode);
                bass.start();
                oscillators.push(bass);
                
                // Drum beat
                playDrum();
                
                chordIndex++;
                if (isPlaying) {
                    setTimeout(playChord, 2000);
                }
            }
            
            function playDrum() {
                const noise = audioContext.createBufferSource();
                const noiseBuffer = audioContext.createBuffer(1, audioContext.sampleRate * 0.1, audioContext.sampleRate);
                const output = noiseBuffer.getChannelData(0);
                
                for (let i = 0; i < noiseBuffer.length; i++) {
                    output[i] = Math.random() * 2 - 1;
                }
                
                noise.buffer = noiseBuffer;
                
                const noiseGain = audioContext.createGain();
                noiseGain.gain.value = 0.3;
                noiseGain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.01, audioContext.currentTime + 0.1);
                
                const filter = audioContext.createBiquadFilter();
                filter.type = 'lowpass';
                filter.frequency.value = 150;
                
                noise.connect(filter);
                filter.connect(noiseGain);
                noiseGain.connect(audioContext.destination);
                noise.start();
            }
            
            playChord();
        }
        
        function enterSite() {
            document.getElementById('intro-overlay').style.display = 'none';
            isPlaying = true;
            createEpicMusic();
            document.getElementById('music-btn').textContent = '';
            document.getElementById('sound-wave').classList.remove('paused');
        }
        
        function toggleMusic() {
            if (isPlaying) {
                isPlaying = false;
                oscillators.forEach(osc => {
                    try { osc.stop(); } catch(e) {}
                });
                document.getElementById('music-btn').textContent = '';
                document.getElementById('sound-wave').classList.add('paused');
            } else {
                isPlaying = true;
                createEpicMusic();
                document.getElementById('music-btn').textContent = '';
                document.getElementById('sound-wave').classList.remove('paused');
            }
        }
        
        // ===== LANGUAGE SWITCHER =====
        function setLang(lang) {
            document.documentElement.dir = lang === 'ar' ? 'rtl' : 'ltr';
            document.documentElement.lang = lang;
            
            document.querySelectorAll('.lang-btn').forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
            event.target.classList.add('active');
            
            document.querySelectorAll('[data-' + lang + ']').forEach(el => {
                el.textContent = el.getAttribute('data-' + lang);
            });
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>
'@
